	<script type="text/javascript" src="/template/reader/web/js/jquery.qrcode.min.js"></script>
	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>

	<script>
        function setClassContent() {
            var length = 20; // 生成字符串的长度
            var characters = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; // 可选的字符集合
            var randomString = '';

            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length);
                randomString += characters.charAt(randomIndex);
            }

            var keywordContent = ['看','小','说','就到','盐', '神', '阁','小','说','网']; // 要插入的关键词内容
            var insertedString = insertKeywordContent(randomString, keywordContent);

            return insertedString;
        }

        function insertKeywordContent(string, keywords) {
            var insertedString = '';
            var keywordIndex = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < string.length; i += 3) {
                insertedString += string.slice(i, i + 3);

                if (keywordIndex < keywords.length) {
                    insertedString += keywords[keywordIndex];
                    keywordIndex++;
                }
            }

            return insertedString;
        }
        function generateRandomParagraphs(count) {
            for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                // 创建<p>标签
                var paragraph = document.createElement('p');
                
                // 设置<p>标签的内容
                paragraph.textContent = setClassContent()+"_www_ysg0_com";
                
                // 将<p>标签添加到目标元素中
                document.getElementsByClassName("read-content j_readContent")[0].appendChild(paragraph);
            }
        }
        
        var count = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
        generateRandomParagraphs(count);
        // addRandomClass('read-content j_readContent');
    </script>
